All Windows-specific code is guarded with `#if defined(PLATFORM_WINDOWS)`. **`InitialiseThreadAffinity()`**: new `ThreadManager` method queries LP count, logs the full engine thread → logical-processor layout table at startup, and warns when requested LPs exceed system capacity. **Fixed**: `TM_LOG_LEVEL` and `TM_LOG_DEBUG` macros were previously defined recursively (calling themselves), causing undefined behaviour when `_DEBUG_THREADMANAGER_` was enabled; corrected to call `debug.logLevelMessage()` and `debug.logDebugMessage()` respectively. **`main.cpp`**: `threadManager.InitialiseThreadAffinity()` called immediately after `DetectAndLogAudioDevices()` and before any `SetThread()` invocation.
- *See: [`ThreadManager.h`](ThreadManager.h), [`ThreadManager.cpp`](ThreadManager.cpp), [`main.cpp`](main.cpp)*

- **Feature — ConsoleWindow: cursor blink and built-in command processing** (`ConsoleWindow.h`, `ConsoleWindow.cpp`):
  The command-bar cursor (`_`) now flashes on/off every 1 second using `std::chrono::steady_clock` timing in `RenderContent()`. The cursor is always forced visible when the console opens (`Toggle()`) and when the user types or deletes a character (`OnCharInput()`, `OnBackspace()`), ensuring the cursor never disappears mid-edit. Command submission (Enter key, KEY UP) now routes through a new `ProcessCommand()` method before calling the external `m_commandCallback`. `ProcessCommand` strips leading/trailing whitespace, lowercases the input for case-insensitive matching, and dispatches built-in commands first. Built-in commands added: **`clear`** — calls `Clear()` to erase all buffer lines. If the input is not a built-in and no `m_commandCallback` is registered, the console prints `> Command [<input>] is unknown.` (as `ConsoleLineColor::Warning`). External callbacks registered via `SetCommandCallback()` receive the original trimmed (but not lowercased) command string and continue to take full responsibility for non-built-in commands when set.
- *See: [`ConsoleWindow.h`](ConsoleWindow.h), [`ConsoleWindow.cpp`](ConsoleWindow.cpp)*

- **Feature — ConsoleWindow: DEBUG-only built-in commands** (`ConsoleWindow.cpp`):
  Three new built-in commands are compiled in under `#if defined(_DEBUG)` only and are therefore completely absent from Release builds. **`test load dialog`** — calls `GUIManager::CreateLoadDialog()` with a generic title, `C:\` initial path, and an `*.*` filter; the `onConfirm` callback prints the chosen file path to the console as a Normal line; the `onCancel` callback prints `Load dialog cancelled.` as a Warning; an immediate Warning is printed if `m_guiMgr` is null. **`test save dialog`** — equivalent test for `GUIManager::CreateSaveDialog()`, pre-filling the filename as `untitled.txt`; callbacks mirror the load dialog behaviour. **`help`** — opens `help.dat` in binary mode via `fopen`, sizes the file with `fseek`/`ftell`, allocates a raw `char[]` buffer with `new`, reads the entire file with `fread`, closes the handle, then walks the buffer emitting one `AddLine()` call per text line (CRLF- and LF-aware); after all lines are emitted the buffer is explicitly released with `delete[]` and nulled. Appropriate error lines are printed for a missing or empty file.
- *See: [`ConsoleWindow.cpp`](ConsoleWindow.cpp)*

- **Visual — GUIConfigWindow: full UI overhaul — 3D drop shadow, gradient titlebar, rectangular close button, wide 3D scrollbar, clip fix** (`GUIConfigWindow.cpp`, `GUIManager.cpp`):
  Complete visual rework of the System Configuration window and its associated controls to match the quality of `GUIFileDialog`.  **Window drop shadow**: a `6,8` offset semi-transparent black rectangle drawn first in `onCustomRender` gives the window depth against the scene. **5-zone gradient titlebar** (no images): renders five horizontal colour bands — top sheen `(90,130,225)`, upper highlight `(55,88,175)`, mid-tone transition `(28,40,92)`, dark base `(12,16,40)`, and lower shadow `(5,8,22)` — plus a top glass line, a hard bottom divider, and a raised outer bevel on the left/top/right edges, producing a strong 3D convex look. **Title text** is now left-aligned at `x+8` and vertically centred within the titlebar (replaces `DrawMyTextCentered`). **Rectangular close button** (no images): replaces the previous filled circle; rendered as a `22×24` red 3D raised button (two-tone gradient body, inner glass strip, four-edge bevel) with a `×` character centred; the `btn_circleclose` hit-area GUIControl updated to match the new position and size. **Scrollbar** width increased from 12 px to 18 px; the scrollbar track is now drawn with a full sunken-bevel border (dark top-left, lighter bottom-right, inner trough); the thumb gains a two-tone gradient body, a raised four-edge bevel, and three horizontal grip dashes centred in the thumb when there is content to scroll. **Clipping region**: `m_clipSize.y` reduced by an additional 4 px (`CONT_H - 8` instead of `CONT_H - 4`) to eliminate a 4-pixel content bleed-through at the bottom of the content area on the Video tab. **ToggleSlider** redesigned: OFF track now neutral grey `(52,54,62)` instead of dark red; ON track vivid green `(22,130,38)`; knob is white for ON and light steel-grey `(182,186,200)` for OFF (matching an iOS-style toggle image), with a four-edge raised bevel, a top glass shine strip, and a centre-groove notch. **HSlider** redesigned: track depth increased to 8 px with a full 3D sunken bevel (dark outer edges, lighter inner bevel, recessed trough); progress fill uses a two-tone blue gradient (lighter upper half); knob width increased to 16 px, rendered with a two-tone body gradient, a four-edge raised bevel (bright top/left, dark bottom/right), an inner second-level bevel, and three paired vertical grip notches as a tactile centre indicator; gold flash on active drag, blue gradient otherwise.
- *See: [`GUIConfigWindow.cpp`](GUIConfigWindow.cpp), [`GUIManager.cpp`](GUIManager.cpp)*

- **Visual — GUIConfigWindow: 7-point UI quality pass** (`GUIConfigWindow.cpp`, `GUIManager.cpp`):
  Further refinements to the System Configuration window. **10-zone fine gradient titlebar**: the previous 5-zone gradient replaced with a 10-zone pixel-accurate gradient — zones step from near-black navy at base `(6,8,28)` through dark indigo, cobalt, royal blue, intense sky-blue, and a bright glass cap `(195,225,255)` at the top 4%, with matching top glass line `(220,240,255,120)` and outer bevel edges, producing an intense fine-detail gradient. **Title text bold and centred**: `DrawMyText` replaced with `DrawMyTextCentered(..., bold=true)` using the full titlebar width (minus close button clearance), so the title is both horizontally and vertically centred and rendered bold on all pipelines. **Close button bold X**: the `×` Unicode symbol replaced with a plain bold `L"X"` rendered via `DrawMyTextCentered(..., bold=true)` at 13 pt, giving a cleaner, heavier close glyph. **HSlider grip bars shifted 2 px left**: the three vertical grip notches are now offset at `knobCentreX - 5.0f` (was `-3.0f`) for better visual balance on the knob. **Vertical scrollbar gold only**: thumb colour changed from blue `(105,118,185)` to an amber-gold two-tone gradient (idle `(210,178,40)` / `(165,128,12)`, active `(235,205,50)` / `(190,148,18)`); bevel edges updated to gold tones; grip dash highlight now warm-gold `(255,245,180,55)`. **Scrollbar thumb flashes when active**: a `lastScrollClick` timestamp (`std::shared_ptr<std::atomic<uint64_t>>`) is updated in `onCustomMouseInput` whenever the scrollbar is clicked/dragged; `onCustomRender` checks if the timestamp is less than 600 ms old and alternates between bright flash gold `(255,235,80)` and active gold `(235,205,50)` at 220 ms intervals via `GetTickCount64()`. **Restart notification window 3D redesign**: window enlarged to 480×188 px; background set transparent and the entire frame rendered by `onCustomRender` — window drop shadow (+7,+10 offset), double-level raised bevel outer border (outer `(95,105,145)` highlight / `(4,5,10)` shadow, inner `(68,78,112)` / `(8,9,16)`), and a classic solid 3D gradient titlebar (dark navy base with a 45%-wide brighter blue upper band and a 2 px top shine strip), with the title `"Video Settings - Restart Required"` drawn bold and centred via `DrawMyTextCentered`; button `bold=true` applied directly rather than via `#if defined(__USE_OPENGL__)` guards; restart countdown timer increased from 10 to **30 seconds**.
- *See: [`GUIConfigWindow.cpp`](GUIConfigWindow.cpp), [`GUIManager.cpp`](GUIManager.cpp)*

- **Visual — GUIManager: ToggleSlider circular knob** (`GUIManager.cpp`):
  Toggle button knob changed from a rectangle to a true circle using `DrawCircle()` (available on all four render pipelines). `knobW` is now set equal to `knobH` (= `control.size.y - 6.0f`, typically 20 px) so the knob dimensions are square. The knob is drawn as: a drop-shadow circle (+1.5,+1.5 offset, alpha 110), a filled body circle (white when ON, light steel-grey when OFF), an inner highlight circle offset upward by 18% of the radius (simulates a dome lit from above), an outer ring stroke via the unfilled `DrawCircle` overload (lighter tint for top-left, darker for bottom-right to suggest a convex surface), and a small gloss highlight circle near the top (radius 28% of knob radius, alpha 85–110). The net effect is a convincing 3D spherical push-button on all pipelines with no rectangle-based corner artefacts.
- *See: [`GUIManager.cpp`](GUIManager.cpp)*

- **Fix — GUIConfigWindow: restart window content was hidden by onCustomRender overdraw** (`GUIConfigWindow.cpp`):
  The restart notification `onCustomRender` callback ran after controls were rendered and filled the entire window body with a solid rectangle, covering the message text, countdown label, and buttons. Fix: window background changed from transparent `(0,0,0,0)` to the solid dark body colour `(18,20,32,252)` so controls paint onto an opaque background; `onCustomRender` now draws only the two-level bevel border edges and the titlebar area gradient on top — it never fills the content area.
- *See: [`GUIConfigWindow.cpp`](GUIConfigWindow.cpp)*

- **Visual — GUIManager: ToggleSlider pill-shaped track + narrower width** (`GUIManager.cpp`, `GUIConfigWindow.cpp`):
  The toggle track is now a pill / capsule shape: two filled circles (radius = half track height) centred at each end, joined by a filled rectangle across the middle. Sunken bevel applied with single-pixel unfilled `DrawCircle` rings on each cap and a dark/light 1 px line pair on the straight section. Toggle control width reduced from 90 px to 70 px in `addTogSlider` so the control occupies less horizontal space in each settings row.
- *See: [`GUIManager.cpp`](GUIManager.cpp), [`GUIConfigWindow.cpp`](GUIConfigWindow.cpp)*

- **Visual — GUIConfigWindow: titlebar text left-aligned at 16 pt** (`GUIConfigWindow.cpp`):
  The config window titlebar title was centered horizontally via `DrawMyTextCentered`; changed to `DrawMyText` at `wx+8` so the text is left-aligned. Font size increased from 14 pt to 16 pt. Since `DrawMyText` has no bold parameter, a pseudo-bold effect is achieved by rendering the text twice: once at `x+1` with 160 alpha (widens strokes) and once at `x` at full 255 alpha, producing a visually heavier weight without a dedicated bold path.
- *See: [`GUIConfigWindow.cpp`](GUIConfigWindow.cpp)*

#### June 24, 2026

- **Visual — GUIManager: ToggleSlider — clean pill fill, no caption** (`GUIManager.cpp`):
  Removed the ON/OFF text caption from the toggle control entirely. Removed the unfilled `DrawCircle` outline rings on each cap and the dark/light 1 px bevel lines on the straight section — these were bleeding into the middle of the control due to the circle radius extending into the rectangular region. Draw order corrected: middle rectangle is now painted first as the base, then the two cap circles are painted on top to cleanly overdraw the rectangular corners, producing an artefact-free pill shape on all four render pipelines.
- *See: [`GUIManager.cpp`](GUIManager.cpp)*

- **Visual — GUIConfigWindow: toggle width reduced, restart window narrowed, clip rect adjusted, smooth titlebar gradients** (`GUIConfigWindow.cpp`):
  Toggle control width reduced from 70 px to 52 px in `addTogSlider`. Restart notification window width reduced by 40 px (OpenGL: 460 → 420, all other pipelines: 480 → 440). Config window clip region height reduced by 1 px (`CONT_H - 8` → `CONT_H - 9`) to push the bottom clip boundary down one pixel. Both the main config titlebar and the restart notification titlebar replaced their multi-zone blocky gradient implementations with a per-pixel linear-interpolation loop — each horizontal row receives an individually computed colour via piecewise lerp through 10 colour stops (main) and 6 colour stops (restart), producing a perfectly smooth continuous gradient with no visible band boundaries.
- *See: [`GUIConfigWindow.cpp`](GUIConfigWindow.cpp)*

- **UI — Game Menu button spacing tightened** (`GUIWindows.cpp`):
  Reduced the vertical stride between buttons in `CreateGameMenuWindow` from 55 px to 45 px to match the tighter layout of `CreateDifficultyWindow`. Affected buttons: gameplayButton (y+110→y+100), hiscoresButton (y+165→y+145), creditsButton (y+220→y+190), quitButton (y+275→y+235), experimentalButton/debug (y+330→y+280). `configButton` at y+55 is unchanged.
- *See: [`GUIWindows.cpp`](GUIWindows.cpp)*

- **FX — New ImageFadeStrobe effect across all 4 render pipelines** (`DX_FXManager`, `DX12FXManager`, `OpenGLFXManager`, `VULKAN_FXManager`, all 4 RenderFrame files, all 4 Renderer subclasses, `Renderer.h`):
  New repeating alpha-strobe visual effect. Signature: `ImageFadeStrobe(BlitObj2DIndexType type, float fadeOutPercentage, float fadeOverTime)`. `fadeOutPercentage` controls the minimum opacity at the bottom of the strobe (100=fully transparent, 50=half faded). `fadeOverTime` sets the duration in seconds for each half-cycle (fade-out phase and fade-in phase each take this long). The effect loops indefinitely until `StopImageFadeStrobe()` is called; removal occurs cleanly at the end of the next fade-in phase to avoid a visible pop. Up to 10 simultaneous instances are supported. A new pure-virtual `Blit2DObjectToSizeWithAlpha()` method was added to `Renderer.h` and implemented in all 4 renderer subclasses (DX11/DX12 use D2D `DrawBitmap` opacity; OpenGL uses `Render2DQuad` with `MyColor` alpha; Vulkan uses D2D with a Linux/Android fallback). All 4 FXManagers received the `ImageFadeStrobe` FXType, a `StrobePhase` enum, a renderer-specific data struct, and the full set of public/private methods. The TSOO image blit in all 4 render pipelines is now guarded: strobe rendering is used when active, otherwise the normal `Blit2DObjectToSize` path is taken.
- *See: [`GUIWindows.cpp`](GUIWindows.cpp), [`Renderer.h`](Renderer.h), [`DX11Renderer.h`](DX11Renderer.h), [`DX11Renderer.cpp`](DX11Renderer.cpp), [`DX12Renderer.h`](DX12Renderer.h), [`DX12Renderer.cpp`](DX12Renderer.cpp), [`OpenGLRenderer.h`](OpenGLRenderer.h), [`OpenGLRenderer.cpp`](OpenGLRenderer.cpp), [`VULKAN_Renderer.h`](VULKAN_Renderer.h), [`VULKAN_Renderer.cpp`](VULKAN_Renderer.cpp), [`DX_FXManager.h`](DX_FXManager.h), [`DX_FXManager.cpp`](DX_FXManager.cpp), [`DX12FXManager.h`](DX12FXManager.h), [`DX12FXManager.cpp`](DX12FXManager.cpp), [`OpenGLFXManager.h`](OpenGLFXManager.h), [`OpenGLFXManager.cpp`](OpenGLFXManager.cpp), [`VULKAN_FXManager.h`](VULKAN_FXManager.h), [`VULKAN_FXManager.cpp`](VULKAN_FXManager.cpp), [`DXRenderFrame.cpp`](DXRenderFrame.cpp), [`DX12RenderFrame.cpp`](DX12RenderFrame.cpp), [`OpenGLRenderFrame.cpp`](OpenGLRenderFrame.cpp), [`VULKAN_RenderFrame.cpp`](VULKAN_RenderFrame.cpp)*

- **Windowing — Exclusive fullscreen with resolution restore on shutdown (all 4 pipelines)** (`OpenGLRenderer.h`, `OpenGLRenderer.cpp`, `VULKAN_Renderer.h`, `VULKAN_Renderer.cpp`):
  When `displayMode == 0` (fullscreen), all four render pipelines now launch into true exclusive fullscreen mode via `ChangeDisplaySettingsW(&dm, CDS_FULLSCREEN)` and properly restore the desktop resolution on shutdown via `ChangeDisplaySettingsW(nullptr, 0)`. DX11 was already correct. Vulkan's `SetFullExclusive` was previously a no-op that only called `Resize()` — replaced with the full `ChangeDisplaySettingsW` implementation matching the DX11/DX12 pattern. OpenGL already called `ChangeDisplaySettingsW` in `SetFullExclusive` but had no tracking flag and did not restore on `Cleanup()`. Both OpenGL and Vulkan renderers now carry `m_isExclusiveFullscreen` and `m_originalDesktopMode` members; `Cleanup()` checks the flag and restores before resource teardown. `SetWindowedScreen()` in both renderers also clears the flag when transitioning back to windowed at runtime.
- *See: [`OpenGLRenderer.h`](OpenGLRenderer.h), [`OpenGLRenderer.cpp`](OpenGLRenderer.cpp), [`VULKAN_Renderer.h`](VULKAN_Renderer.h), [`VULKAN_Renderer.cpp`](VULKAN_Renderer.cpp)*

- **Windowing — Non-resizable Windowed and Borderless windows across all pipelines** (`main.cpp`, `OpenGLRenderer.cpp`, `VULKAN_Renderer.cpp`):
  In Windowed and Borderless modes the application window can no longer be resized. `WS_WINDOWED_FIXED` constant defined (`WS_OVERLAPPED | WS_CAPTION | WS_SYSMENU | WS_MINIMIZEBOX`) removes `WS_THICKFRAME` (drag-resize border) and `WS_MAXIMIZEBOX`. All three `CreateWindowEx` / `AdjustWindowRect` calls in `main.cpp` switched to this style. A `WM_GETMINMAXINFO` handler added to the Win32 message pump locks the min and max track size to the configured resolution (accounting for frame chrome in Windowed mode), providing a second line of defence against OS-level resize attempts. `SetWindowedScreen()` in both OpenGL and Vulkan renderers updated to restore the same non-resizable style instead of `WS_OVERLAPPEDWINDOW`.
- *See: [`main.cpp`](main.cpp), [`OpenGLRenderer.cpp`](OpenGLRenderer.cpp), [`VULKAN_Renderer.cpp`](VULKAN_Renderer.cpp)*

- **Windowing — Config window minimum selectable resolution raised to 800x600** (`GUIConfigWindow.cpp`):
  `ScanDisplayModes()` now skips any display mode whose width is below 800 or height is below 600. This prevents resolutions such as 640x480 or smaller from appearing in the configuration window resolution list.
- *See: [`GUIConfigWindow.cpp`](GUIConfigWindow.cpp)*

- **OpenGL — ImageFadeStrobe background-blit duplicate removed** (`OpenGLRenderer.cpp`):
  `RenderBackgroundImage()` in the SCENE_GAMETITLE branch was unconditionally blitting `IMG_TSOO` at full opacity before 3D models rendered. The correct strobe-aware render of that image already exists in the post-3D overlay pass in `OpenGLRenderFrame.cpp`. The premature background blit has been removed; the fireworks pass (`fxManager.RenderFireworks()`) now runs in its place, matching the DX11 pipeline order.
- *See: [`OpenGLRenderer.cpp`](OpenGLRenderer.cpp)*

#### June 25, 2026

- **Performance — DX12: DXGI Frame Latency Waitable Object — Present() made non-blocking** (`DX12Renderer.h`, `DX12Renderer.cpp`, `DX12RenderFrame.cpp`):
  Frame timing analysis (25-frame capture) showed `Present()` consuming an average of 14.046ms per frame (58.8% of total frame time), reducing effective framerate to ~42fps. Root cause: `Present(1, 0)` with no frame latency waitable object blocks the CPU render thread until the next vblank. Fix: swap chain created with `DXGI_SWAP_CHAIN_FLAG_FRAME_LATENCY_WAITABLE_OBJECT` (requires changing `DXGI_SCALING_STRETCH` to `DXGI_SCALING_NONE` — safe since the back buffer always matches window size via `Resize()`). `IDXGISwapChain2::SetMaximumFrameLatency(2)` set after creation; the waitable handle stored in `m_frameLatencyWaitableObject`. A `WaitForSingleObjectEx` call at the start of each frame iteration (before camera update and before the GPU fence wait) replaces the vblank stall that previously lived inside `Present()`. `Present()` now returns immediately, the CPU starts the next frame right away, and DXGI paces delivery via the waitable signal. `ResizeBuffers` updated to preserve the flag. Handle closed in `Cleanup()`. Expected result: `present` timing drops to near 0ms; total frame time reduces to actual render cost (~9ms), enabling 60fps.
- *See: [`DX12Renderer.h`](DX12Renderer.h), [`DX12Renderer.cpp`](DX12Renderer.cpp), [`DX12RenderFrame.cpp`](DX12RenderFrame.cpp)*

- **OpenGL — GUI windows no longer default to 800x600 when config resolution differs** (`OpenGLRenderer.cpp`):
  `OpenGLRenderer::Initialize()` now falls back to `config.myConfig.resolutionWidth/resolutionHeight` when `winMetrics.clientWidth/clientHeight` are zero (i.e. not yet populated at init time). Previously the renderer fell through to the `DEFAULT_WINDOW_WIDTH/HEIGHT = 800/600` class defaults, causing all GUI windows (which centre using `iOrigWidth`/`iOrigHeight`) to position as if the viewport were 800x600 regardless of the actual configured resolution.
- *See: [`OpenGLRenderer.cpp`](OpenGLRenderer.cpp)*

- **DX12 — RenderGamePlay guarded by bLoaderTaskFinished in SCENE_GAMETITLE** (`DX12RenderFrame.cpp`):
  `RenderGamePlay(deltaTime)` in STEP 8 SCENE_GAMETITLE was being called before the loader-finished check, inconsistent with the DX11 and OpenGL pipelines. Moved inside the `bLoaderTaskFinished.load()` guard alongside the animation update, ensuring 3D models are never submitted for rendering before async loading completes.
- *See: [`DX12RenderFrame.cpp`](DX12RenderFrame.cpp)*

- **All Pipelines — Fullscreen Exclusive viewport fixed to use back-buffer dimensions** (`DXRenderFrame.cpp`, `DX12RenderFrame.cpp`, `OpenGLRenderFrame.cpp`):
  In fullscreen exclusive mode the DX11, DX12, and OpenGL render frames were deriving the 3D viewport size from `winMetrics.monitorFullArea` (`GetMonitorInfo.rcMonitor`), which lives in OS virtual-screen coordinates and can be stale after a display-mode switch (e.g. it may report the native monitor resolution while the swap chain is running at a non-native configured resolution). The 2D / D2D / blitting code in the same frames always used `iOrigWidth`/`iOrigHeight` (set authoritatively by `Resize()` inside `SetFullExclusive()`), so the 3D viewport and the 2D coordinate space disagreed — causing movies, the loading screen, `SCENE_GAMETITLE`, and `SCENE_GAMEPLAY` to render with missing imagery, wrong offsets, or misaligned elements. All three render frames now derive both the 3D viewport and their `m_renderTargetWidth`/`m_renderTargetHeight` exclusively from `iOrigWidth`/`iOrigHeight`, keeping the two coordinate spaces in sync for every display mode. The Vulkan render frame was already correct (it uses `m_swapchainExtent` directly) and was not changed.
- *See: [`DXRenderFrame.cpp`](DXRenderFrame.cpp), [`DX12RenderFrame.cpp`](DX12RenderFrame.cpp), [`OpenGLRenderFrame.cpp`](OpenGLRenderFrame.cpp)*

- **All Pipelines — WM_SIZE rewritten; fullscreen winMetrics set from renderer back-buffer; Vulkan & OpenGL bSettingFullScreen guards added** (`main.cpp`, `VULKAN_Renderer.cpp`, `OpenGLRenderer.cpp`):
  Root-cause analysis showed three compounding issues causing all four pipelines to render incorrectly in fullscreen exclusive mode. **(1)** `sysUtils.GetWindowMetrics()` was called immediately after `SetFullExclusive()` and could return stale OS dimensions (from `GetMonitorInfo.rcMonitor`, `GetWindowRect`) before the display-mode switch had fully committed, giving cameras, the GUI, and the FX system a mismatched coordinate space. Fixed by populating `winMetrics` directly from `renderer->iOrigWidth/iOrigHeight` — the authoritative back-buffer dimensions confirmed by `Resize()` — with a config-value fallback, eliminating any reliance on timing-sensitive WinAPI reads. **(2)** Vulkan's `SetFullExclusive()` called `SetWindowPos()` without setting `bSettingFullScreen`, so the WM_SIZE fired during that call was not suppressed and could trigger a concurrent metrics sync against an inconsistent renderer state; `bSettingFullScreen` guards added around `SetWindowPos + Resize()`. OpenGL's `SetFullExclusive()` had the same omission and additionally relied on `GetSystemMetrics(SM_CXSCREEN/SM_CYSCREEN)` inside `SetFullScreen()` which can read stale native-resolution values immediately after `ChangeDisplaySettingsW`; both guards and an explicit `iOrigWidth/iOrigHeight` override added. **(3)** The `WM_SIZE` handler was rewritten: since user window-resizing is not permitted, the handler now only handles minimise/restore and a lightweight `winMetrics` sync from renderer dims. All the former resize path logic (ThreadLockHelper, WaitToFinishThenPauseThread, Resize, ResumeLoader, camera save/restore) has been removed — those operations are handled entirely within the renderer's own transition methods (`SetFullExclusive`, `SetWindowedScreen`, `Resize`).
- *See: [`main.cpp`](main.cpp), [`VULKAN_Renderer.cpp`](VULKAN_Renderer.cpp), [`OpenGLRenderer.cpp`](OpenGLRenderer.cpp)*

- **All Pipelines — Swap chain and render targets seeded from config resolution; SetFullExclusive winMetrics now self-contained** (`DX11Renderer.cpp`, `DX12Renderer.cpp`, `OpenGLRenderer.cpp`, `VULKAN_Renderer.cpp`, `main.cpp`):
  Root cause: each renderer's `Initialize()` was seeding `iOrigWidth/iOrigHeight` from `winMetrics.clientWidth/clientHeight` (windowed dimensions at that point), so the swap chain and all render targets were created at windowed size. Fix: all four renderers now seed `iOrigWidth/iOrigHeight` and `m_renderTargetWidth/m_renderTargetHeight` from `config.myConfig.resolutionWidth/Height`. `SetFullExclusive()` in all four renderers now also updates `winMetrics` directly from the confirmed back-buffer dimensions after the mode switch, removing the manual population block that previously lived in `main.cpp`. The `SetFullExclusive()` call itself remains in `main.cpp`'s `default:` case — an attempt to move it inside `Initialize()` caused a deadlock because DXGI's `SetFullscreenState(TRUE)` pumps the Windows message queue synchronously while `s_renderMutex` is held, and any WindowProc re-entry on the same thread would deadlock the non-reentrant mutex.
- *See: [`DX11Renderer.cpp`](DX11Renderer.cpp), [`DX12Renderer.cpp`](DX12Renderer.cpp), [`OpenGLRenderer.cpp`](OpenGLRenderer.cpp), [`VULKAN_Renderer.cpp`](VULKAN_Renderer.cpp), [`main.cpp`](main.cpp)*

- **All Pipelines — winMetrics pre-seeded from config resolution in fullscreen mode** (`main.cpp`):
  `sysUtils.GetWindowMetrics(hwnd, winMetrics)` fires immediately after `CreateWindowEx` while the window is still at its initial windowed size (e.g. 800×600 client, 816×639 outer). In fullscreen exclusive mode (`displayMode == 2`) this means every subsystem initialised before `SetFullExclusive()` — including `renderer->Initialize()`, shader manager, GUI — saw stale windowed client dimensions via `winMetrics`. Fix: immediately after the `GetWindowMetrics` call, when `displayMode == 2`, override `winMetrics.width/height/clientWidth/clientHeight` from `config.myConfig.resolutionWidth/Height` and zero `borderWidth`/`titleBarHeight`. `SetFullExclusive()` re-confirms the actual back-buffer dimensions and overwrites `winMetrics` a second time at the end of the transition, so the final state is always authoritative.
- *See: [`main.cpp`](main.cpp)*

- **Performance — DX12: DX12FXManager hot-path optimizations** (`DX12FXManager.cpp`):
  Seven targeted optimizations applied to the FX rendering hot paths to reduce per-frame CPU cost:
  **(1) RemoveCompletedEffects** — replaced the per-call `std::vector<size_t> indicesToRemove` + O(n²) reverse-erase loop with a single-pass `std::remove_if` + `erase`, eliminating a heap allocation and multiple index-shift operations each frame.
  **(2) UpdateWarpDotTunnel — stack array** — replaced the per-frame `std::vector<int> order` heap allocation (used for camera look-target sort) with a fixed-size `int order[100]` stack array; density is clamped to [1,100] so this is always safe.
  **(3) FAST_MATH — WarpDotTunnel ring respawn (forward and reverse)** — replaced `sinf(phase)` / `cosf(phase)` with `FAST_MATH.FastSinCos` for ring bornCx/bornCy recalculation on ring wrap. Applied to both the forward-travel and reverse-travel respawn branches.
  **(4) FAST_MATH — WarpDotTunnel initial ring spawn (CreateWarpDotTunnel)** — replaced `sinf` / `cosf` in the initial ring-placement loop with `FAST_MATH.FastSinCos`.
  **(5) FAST_MATH — Starfield reverse-respawn (UpdateStarfield)** — replaced `cosf(a2)` / `sinf(a2)` with `FAST_MATH.FastSinCos` for the reverse-mode particle velocity recalculation on depth reset.
  **(6) FAST_MATH — Starfield initial placement (CreateStarfield)** — replaced `cosf(angle)` / `sinf(angle)` with `FAST_MATH.FastSinCos` for the circular-spread spawn position calculation.
  **(7) DX12Renderer\* pointer hoisted in all per-pixel render loops** — `RenderParticles`, `RenderStarfield`, `RenderWarpDotTunnel`, and `DrawFireworksPixels` previously called `GetDX12RendererFast()` (which calls `renderer.get()`) once per particle/star/dot/pixel. Pointer now resolved once per function call, with early-return if null; hot loops call `dx12->Blit2DColoredPixelFast` directly.
  **(8) ApplyScroller tile-wrap — power-of-2 bitmask** — the `currentXOffset` / `currentYOffset` modulo-wrap used two integer divisions per axis per frame. Now detects power-of-2 tile dimensions (the common case: 64, 128, 256) and replaces the division with a single AND bitmask (`x & (n-1)`); non-power-of-2 sizes fall back to the original modulo.
- *See: [`DX12FXManager.cpp`](DX12FXManager.cpp)*

- **All Pipelines — Process DPI awareness set before window creation; fullscreen m_renderTargetWidth/Height sync fixed** (`main.cpp`, `DX11Renderer.cpp`, `OpenGLRenderer.cpp`, `DX12Renderer.cpp`, `VULKAN_Renderer.cpp`):
  Root cause of "only top-left quarter visible in fullscreen on high-DPI monitors": the process had no DPI awareness declaration, so Windows DPI-virtualised all Win32 APIs (window sizes, `GetClientRect`, `AdjustWindowRect`) to return logical pixels while DXGI/OpenGL/Vulkan surface allocation operates in physical pixels. On a 200% scaled display this produces a 2× dimension mismatch. Fix: `ConfigureProcessDpiAwareness()` added to `main.cpp` and called immediately after the Windows version check, before any `RegisterClassEx`/`CreateWindowEx`/`AdjustWindowRect` call. It attempts `DPI_AWARENESS_CONTEXT_PER_MONITOR_AWARE_V2` (Win10 1703+), falls back to `DPI_AWARENESS_CONTEXT_PER_MONITOR_AWARE`, then to legacy `SetProcessDPIAware()`. Secondary fix: `DX11Renderer::SetFullExclusive()` was updating `iOrigWidth/iOrigHeight` from the DXGI `closestMode` but never syncing `m_renderTargetWidth/m_renderTargetHeight`, so the per-frame viewport and `DrawMyTextStyled` centring path used stale windowed dimensions for the rest of the session. `m_renderTargetWidth/m_renderTargetHeight` now set from `closestMode` immediately after `iOrigWidth/iOrigHeight`. Same omission fixed in `OpenGLRenderer::SetFullExclusive()` — `m_renderTargetWidth/m_renderTargetHeight` now synced from `iOrigWidth/iOrigHeight` after the override assignment. DX12 and Vulkan already route through `Resize()` which handles both fields. Diagnostic logging added to all four `SetFullExclusive()` implementations (guarded by renderer-specific `_DEBUG_*` macros) reporting DPI, window/client rect, config resolution, back-buffer size, and GL/DXGI viewport/extent after each successful transition.
- *See: [`main.cpp`](main.cpp), [`DX11Renderer.cpp`](DX11Renderer.cpp), [`OpenGLRenderer.cpp`](OpenGLRenderer.cpp), [`DX12Renderer.cpp`](DX12Renderer.cpp), [`VULKAN_Renderer.cpp`](VULKAN_Renderer.cpp)*

- **DX11 — ChangeDisplaySettingsEx moved before mutex acquisition to fix deadlock and switch display mode** (`DX11Renderer.cpp`):
  Two sequential bugs were fixed. (1) Resolution mismatch: `SetFullscreenState(TRUE)` without a prior display-mode switch caused DXGI to take exclusive ownership at the monitor's native resolution (e.g. 1768x992), with the 1024x768 back buffer scaled to fill it. Root cause: the swap chain uses `DXGI_SWAP_EFFECT_FLIP_SEQUENTIAL`; MSDN prohibits `DXGI_SWAP_CHAIN_FLAG_ALLOW_MODE_SWITCH` with flip-sequential, so DXGI cannot change the display mode via `ResizeTarget`/`ResizeBuffers`. Fix: `ChangeDisplaySettingsEx(CDS_FULLSCREEN)` physically switches the monitor before DXGI takes ownership, matching the existing OpenGL/Vulkan approach. (2) Deadlock: initial placement of `ChangeDisplaySettingsEx` inside `s_renderMutex` caused a cross-lock deadlock — `ChangeDisplaySettingsEx` pumps `WM_DISPLAYCHANGE` internally; DXGI intercepts that broadcast and tries to acquire its own internal swap-chain lock; `SetFullscreenState` (also inside the mutex) then needs that same DXGI lock, creating a circular wait. Fix: `ChangeDisplaySettingsEx` and `EnumDisplaySettings` (to save the original mode for restoration) are now both called BEFORE the `std::lock_guard<std::mutex>` acquisition so all DXGI display-change processing completes while the mutex is free.
- *See: [`DX11Renderer.cpp`](DX11Renderer.cpp)*

- **All Pipelines — Unified FXManager.h / FXManager.cpp replacing all four pipeline-specific FX managers** (`FXManager.h`, `FXManager.cpp`):
  All four existing FX managers (DX11: `DX_FXManager`, DX12: `DX12FXManager`, OpenGL: `OpenGLFXManager`, Vulkan: `VULKAN_FXManager`) have been unified into a single pair of files. Strict `#if defined(__USE_DIRECTX_11__) / __USE_DIRECTX_12__ / __USE_OPENGL__ / __USE_VULKAN__` conditional compilation directives isolate all pipeline-specific code so that analysis, fixes, and future optimisations can be applied across all four renderers from a single location. The DX12FXManager is the reference gold standard for structure and optimisations. Key changes applied to all pipelines: **(1) FAST_MATH.FastSinCos()** replaces all `sinf()`/`cosf()` calls in starfield, WarpDotTunnel, fireworks, and particle explosion. **(2) Bitmask tile-wrap** — `ApplyScroller` detects power-of-2 tile dimensions and replaces the integer-division modulo with a single AND bitmask (`offset & (n-1)`); signed-safe fallback for non-power-of-2. **(3) Fibonacci sphere distribution** used for fireworks explosion particle burst directions (uniform sphere coverage via golden-angle / `(2i+1)/N` cosTheta formula). **(4) Pending-effects deferred push** — `AddEffect()` defers to `m_pendingEffects` while `bIsRendering` is true; flushed atomically at end of each `Render()` foreground pass to prevent iterator invalidation. **(5) FX_LOCK() macro** resolves to `std::lock_guard<std::recursive_mutex>` on OpenGL (required because `IsFadeActive()` is const and must lock) and `std::lock_guard<std::mutex>` on all other pipelines. **(6) OpenGL lazy shader creation** — `CreateFadeShaderProgram()` deferred to first `RenderFullScreenQuad()` call because `wglMakeCurrent` transfers the GL context to the render thread after `Initialize()` returns. **(7) WarpTunnelData compile-time constants** differ per pipeline family via `#if` in the struct definition: DX12/DX11 use 900/80/0.85/4.0 (distance/speed/wave/smooth), OpenGL/Vulkan use 800/60/0.5/3.0. **(8) Vulkan `ApplyColorFader`** obtains `VkCommandBuffer` internally via `vkr->GetCurrentCommandBuffer()` rather than requiring callers to pass it. File is 2891 lines (`FXManager.cpp`) and 822 lines (`FXManager.h`), designed to be merged as a direct replacement for the four legacy files.
- *See: [`FXManager.h`](FXManager.h), [`FXManager.cpp`](FXManager.cpp)*

- **Debug — F12 per-frame render timing capture system across all four pipelines** (`Renderer.h`, `DXRenderFrame.cpp`, `DX12RenderFrame.cpp`, `OpenGLRenderFrame.cpp`, `VULKAN_RenderFrame.cpp`, `KBHandlersCode.cpp`):
  `RenderTimingSample` struct added to `Renderer.h` captures per-phase timings for each render frame: `waitPreviousMs` (GPU fence / swap-image acquire), `resetMs` (command-list reset), `backgroundPrePassMs`, `commandRecordMs` (3D scene record), `execute3DMs` (GPU submit), `d2dOverlayMs`, `presentMs`, and `totalMs`. A `#if defined(_DEBUG)` circular ring buffer of 25 frames (`m_timingSamples`, `m_timingWriteIndex`, `m_timingSampleCount`) is stored in `Renderer` with `RecordTimingSample()` appending each completed frame. `BeginTimingCapture()` resets the ring and sets `bTimingCaptureActive`; `EndTimingCaptureAndLog()` clears the flag then dumps per-frame rows plus per-phase averages via `Debug::logDebugMessage`. `ToggleTimingCapture()` switches between the two. `KBHandlersCode.cpp` F12 key-up: on `SCENE_GAMETITLE` (debug builds only) calls `renderer->ToggleTimingCapture()`; on `SCENE_GAMEPLAY` keeps the existing wireframe toggle. All four render frames instrument their major phases with `bCollectTiming` guards and call `RecordTimingSample` on frame end. An OSD message "=> Timing Performance: MONITORING / OFF" is displayed for 5 seconds after each toggle.
- *See: [`Renderer.h`](Renderer.h), [`DXRenderFrame.cpp`](DXRenderFrame.cpp), [`DX12RenderFrame.cpp`](DX12RenderFrame.cpp), [`OpenGLRenderFrame.cpp`](OpenGLRenderFrame.cpp), [`VULKAN_RenderFrame.cpp`](VULKAN_RenderFrame.cpp), [`KBHandlersCode.cpp`](KBHandlersCode.cpp)*

- **DX12 — Native DX12 3D shader path: SM6 / FL12 capability gate with dual shader set** (`DX12Renderer.cpp`, `DX12Renderer.h`, `Assets/Shaders/DX12NativeModelVertex.hlsl`, `Assets/Shaders/DX12NativeModelPixel.hlsl`):
  `CreateDevice()` now queries `D3D12_FEATURE_SHADER_MODEL` (probing SM 6.0) and stores the result in `m_shaderModel`. `bUseNativeDX12Calls` atomic bool is set `true` only when `m_maxFeatureLevel >= D3D_FEATURE_LEVEL_12_0` AND `m_shaderModel >= D3D_SHADER_MODEL_6_0` — the engine's gate for the native DX12 3D pipeline. `IsNativeDX12Supported()` public query method added. GPU capability log enhanced with feature level, shader model, and native flag. `CreatePipelineState()` uses a new `loadShaderBlob()` helper lambda: when `bUseNativeDX12Calls` is true it tries `DX12NativeModelVShader.cso`/`DX12NativeModelPShader.cso` with automatic fallback to the proven FXC pair; FL11_x adapters always use `ModelVShader.cso`/`ModelPShader.cso`. Two new HLSL sources added: `Assets/Shaders/DX12NativeModelVertex.hlsl` and `Assets/Shaders/DX12NativeModelPixel.hlsl`, compiled to `DX12NativeModelVShader.cso`/`DX12NativeModelPShader.cso`.
- *See: [`DX12Renderer.cpp`](DX12Renderer.cpp), [`DX12Renderer.h`](DX12Renderer.h), [`Assets/Shaders/DX12NativeModelVertex.hlsl`](Assets/Shaders/DX12NativeModelVertex.hlsl), [`Assets/Shaders/DX12NativeModelPixel.hlsl`](Assets/Shaders/DX12NativeModelPixel.hlsl)*

- **DX12 — DXGI tearing support detected at swap-chain creation; `ALLOW_TEARING` flag conditionally applied** (`DX12Renderer.cpp`, `DX12Renderer.h`):
  `CreateSwapChain()` queries `IDXGIFactory5::CheckFeatureSupport(DXGI_FEATURE_PRESENT_ALLOW_TEARING)` before swap-chain creation; result stored in `m_allowTearing`. `DXGI_SWAP_CHAIN_FLAG_ALLOW_TEARING` conditionally OR-ed into `swapChainDesc.Flags` alongside `ALLOW_MODE_SWITCH` and `FRAME_LATENCY_WAITABLE_OBJECT`. The same conditional is applied in `ResizeBuffers()` so the flag is preserved through every resize.
- *See: [`DX12Renderer.cpp`](DX12Renderer.cpp), [`DX12Renderer.h`](DX12Renderer.h)*

- **DX12 — `Blit2DColoredPixelFast()` added as FX hot-path; `Blit2DColoredPixel` delegates to it; DX12FXManager pixel draw helper** (`DX12Renderer.cpp`, `DX12Renderer.h`, `DX12FXManager.cpp`):
  New `Blit2DColoredPixelFast(int x, int y, float pixelSize, const XMFLOAT4& color)` is a lightweight path for FX code already inside a valid `BeginDraw()`/`EndDraw()` pass; it skips the resize-state check, exception frame, and redundant `m_d2dContext` null check of the safe outer function. `Blit2DColoredPixel` now delegates to `Blit2DColoredPixelFast` after its own guards. In `DX12FXManager.cpp` an anonymous-namespace helper `DrawDX12FXPixel()` calls `Blit2DColoredPixelFast()` on a cached `DX12Renderer*`; all particle/star/dot hot-loops use this helper instead of raw `renderer.get()` casts. Fireworks density constants added (`kDX12MaxFireworkRockets=6`, `kDX12FireworkParticles=48`, `kDX12RocketTrailSteps=3`, `kDX12ExplosionTrailSteps=3`) to limit D2D draw-call amplification on the DX11on12 path.
- *See: [`DX12Renderer.cpp`](DX12Renderer.cpp), [`DX12Renderer.h`](DX12Renderer.h), [`DX12FXManager.cpp`](DX12FXManager.cpp)*

- **DX12 — D2D off-screen composite path removed; D2D now draws directly onto the wrapped back buffer** (`DX12Renderer.cpp`, `DX12RenderFrame.cpp`):
  `CreateD2DOffscreenTargets()` and `CreateD2DCompositePSO()` calls removed from both `Initialize()` and `Resize()`. In `RenderFrame()`, `bUseD2DOffscreen` is hardcoded `false` (previously derived from off-screen resource availability). DX12 now matches the DX11 composition pattern: `Direct2D` draws directly onto the `11on12`-wrapped swap-chain back buffer, eliminating one full-screen composite pass and extra resource transitions on every `SCENE_GAMETITLE` frame.
- *See: [`DX12Renderer.cpp`](DX12Renderer.cpp), [`DX12RenderFrame.cpp`](DX12RenderFrame.cpp)*

- **DX12 — `SetFullScreen()` now sets `m_isExclusiveFullscreen = true`** (`DX12Renderer.cpp`):
  The borderless windowed-fullscreen path via `SetFullScreen()` was calling `Resize()` but never setting `m_isExclusiveFullscreen = true`; only `SetFullExclusive()` set the flag. Fixed: `m_isExclusiveFullscreen = true` added after `Resize()` in `SetFullScreen()`, ensuring `Cleanup()` and `SetWindowedScreen()` correctly detect and restore fullscreen state on that code path.
- *See: [`DX12Renderer.cpp`](DX12Renderer.cpp)*

- **Vulkan — `SetFullExclusive()` fully implemented: display mode switch, WS_POPUP window, `bSettingFullScreen` guard, winMetrics sync, diagnostics** (`VULKAN_Renderer.cpp`, `VULKAN_Renderer.h`):
  Previously `SetFullExclusive()` was a near-stub (`IsWindowMode.store(false); return Resize(width, height);`). Now mirrors the DX12 pattern: **(1)** saves `m_originalDesktopMode` via `EnumDisplaySettingsW` before switching. **(2)** `ChangeDisplaySettingsW(CDS_FULLSCREEN)` physically switches the monitor resolution. **(3)** `bSettingFullScreen` set `true` before `SetWindowPos(WS_POPUP)` so any `WM_SIZE` fired during window style change is suppressed. **(4)** `Resize()` updates the swap chain. **(5)** `winMetrics` fully synced from `iOrigWidth/iOrigHeight` (width, height, clientWidth, clientHeight, borders zeroed, `monitorFullArea`/`WorkArea` set) so every subsystem sees a coherent coordinate space after the transition. **(6)** `bSettingFullScreen` cleared. Fullscreen diagnostics log added (guarded by `_DEBUG_VULKANRENDERER_`). `m_isExclusiveFullscreen` and `m_originalDesktopMode` private members added to `VULKAN_Renderer.h`.
- *See: [`VULKAN_Renderer.cpp`](VULKAN_Renderer.cpp), [`VULKAN_Renderer.h`](VULKAN_Renderer.h)*

- **Vulkan — `SetWindowedScreen()` restores display mode and uses non-resizable window style; `Cleanup()` restores on exit** (`VULKAN_Renderer.cpp`):
  `SetWindowedScreen()`: when `m_isExclusiveFullscreen` is true, `ChangeDisplaySettingsW(nullptr, 0)` restores the desktop mode before resizing the window. Window style changed from `WS_OVERLAPPEDWINDOW` to `WS_OVERLAPPED | WS_CAPTION | WS_SYSMENU | WS_MINIMIZEBOX` (non-resizable: no thick border or maximize box), matching the engine's non-resizable windowed policy. `Cleanup()`: if `m_isExclusiveFullscreen` is true at shutdown, `ChangeDisplaySettingsW(nullptr, 0)` restores the desktop resolution, mirroring DX11/DX12 shutdown behaviour.
- *See: [`VULKAN_Renderer.cpp`](VULKAN_Renderer.cpp)*

- **OpenGL — `m_isExclusiveFullscreen` and `m_originalDesktopMode` members added** (`OpenGLRenderer.h`):
  Windows-only private members `bool m_isExclusiveFullscreen = false` and `DEVMODE m_originalDesktopMode = {}` added to `OpenGLRenderer`, mirroring the DX11/DX12/Vulkan fullscreen-tracking pattern for correct state management and desktop mode restoration.
- *See: [`OpenGLRenderer.h`](OpenGLRenderer.h)*

- **Shader — `ModelPixel.hlsl` SampleShadow: near-zero `lightClip.w` guard prevents undefined perspective divide** (`Assets/Shaders/ModelPixel.hlsl`):
  Guard `if (abs(lightClip.w) < 0.00001f) return shadowFactor;` added immediately after the `mul(worldPos, lightViewProj)` transform. Degenerate geometry with `w ≈ 0` previously produced a division by near-zero in the `xyz / w` perspective divide, yielding undefined projection coordinates and potentially incorrect shadow values; such cases now return `1.0f` (fully lit). Multiple early `return 1.0f` statements refactored to use a single `shadowFactor` variable for clarity.
- *See: [`Assets/Shaders/ModelPixel.hlsl`](Assets/Shaders/ModelPixel.hlsl)*

- **Build — Metal renderer scaffold added; `Includes.h` IDE default renderer and platform defines updated** (`Includes.h`, `Metal/`):
  `#define __USE_DIRECTX_11__` fallback for IDE-only (non-CMake) builds commented out. macOS section updated: OpenGL marked "(Now obsolete on newer platforms)"; `__USE_METAL__` placeholder added for newer macOS. iOS section: OpenGL placeholder removed, `__USE_METAL__` substituted. `RENDERER_NAME_W L"Metal"` entry added for `__USE_METAL__`. New `Metal/` directory scaffolded for the future Metal renderer.
- *See: [`Includes.h`](Includes.h)*

- **Models.cpp — DX11-specific `FXManager::CancelEffect/RestartEffect/ChainEffect` removed; now in unified `FXManager.cpp`** (`Models.cpp`):
  Three `FXManager` method implementations (`CancelEffect`, `RestartEffect`, `ChainEffect`) previously defined in `Models.cpp` under a `#if defined(__USE_DIRECTX_11__)` guard have been removed. These methods are now defined in the unified `FXManager.cpp` and apply to all pipelines.
- *See: [`Models.cpp`](Models.cpp)*

- **GUI — Config window display mode list filtered to 800×600 minimum** (`GUIConfigWindow.cpp`):
  `ScanDisplayModes()` now skips any display mode with `dmPelsWidth < 800` or `dmPelsHeight < 600`, preventing sub-SVGA modes from appearing in the config window resolution picker.
- *See: [`GUIConfigWindow.cpp`](GUIConfigWindow.cpp)*

- **GUI — Title bar caption Y-alignment unified; toggle track colours fully opaque; knob highlight layers revised** (`GUIManager.cpp`):
  **(1) Title bar:** both the centred and left-aligned label paths now compute `captionY` from `position.y + size.y − (captionH + captionH * 0.5f)` (where `captionH = lblFontSize * 1.25f`), so captions sit at a consistent height regardless of alignment. The centred variant now measures character widths via `GetCharacterWidth()` and calls `DrawMyText` rather than `DrawMyTextCentered`, matching the left-aligned path precisely. **(2) Toggle track:** alpha changed from 228–250 to 255 (fully opaque) on both ON and OFF states to eliminate circular antialiased-cap blending bands; colours updated to `(34,172,56,255)`/`(24,138,42,255)` (ON green) and `(78,80,88,255)`/`(54,56,64,255)` (OFF grey). **(3) Toggle knob:** ON fill changed from pure white to `(202,230,206,255)` (green-tinted); dual-layer soft highlight (offset upper-left and lower-right circles) replaces the single centred arc; outer ring bevel simplified — shadow `ringSh` circle removed, single `ringHi` circle retained.
- *See: [`GUIManager.cpp`](GUIManager.cpp)*

- **GUI — ESC in SCENE_GAMETITLE now shows a quit-confirmation modal instead of immediate shutdown** (`GUIManager.h`, `GUIWindows.cpp`, `KBHandlersCode.cpp`, `main.cpp`):
  Pressing ESC at the title/menu screen previously executed a direct fade-to-black → `StopMusicPlayback()` → `PostQuitMessage(0)` shutdown sequence with no opportunity to cancel. Replaced by a modal "CONFIRM EXIT" dialog (`CreateQuitConfirmDialog()`): 520×140px centred window using `IMG_WINFRAME1` background, "CONFIRM EXIT" title bar, "You are about to Quit the Game." message, and two buttons. **OK** (near-right): `FadeOutThenCallback` → `StopMusicPlayback` → `bIsShuttingDown` → `PostMessage(hwnd, WM_CLOSE)`. **CANCEL** (far-right): `RemoveWindow` only. `KBHandlersCode.cpp` ESC handler in `SCENE_GAMETITLE` now checks for an existing `QuitConfirmDialog` window (second ESC press dismisses it as a cancel), then checks for GamePlayTypes/Difficulty sub-windows (existing back-navigation behaviour), then calls `CreateQuitConfirmDialog()` as the terminal action. `QUIT_CONFIRM_WINDOW_NAME = "QuitConfirmDialog"` constant added to `GUIWindows.cpp`; `extern` declaration added to `main.cpp`.
- *See: [`GUIManager.h`](GUIManager.h), [`GUIWindows.cpp`](GUIWindows.cpp), [`KBHandlersCode.cpp`](KBHandlersCode.cpp), [`main.cpp`](main.cpp)*
